        wp1_0.phone_number,
        wp1_0.profile_picture_url,
        wp1_0.rejected_at,
        wp1_0.rejected_by,
        wp1_0.rejection_reason,
        s1_0.worker_id,
        s1_1.id,
        s1_1.name,
        wp1_0.status,
        wp1_0.user_id 
    from
        worker_profiles wp1_0 
    left join
        worker_skills s1_0 
            on wp1_0.id=s1_0.worker_id 
    left join
        skills s1_1 
            on s1_1.id=s1_0.skill_id 
    where
        wp1_0.user_id=?
